That nanny is hella strict, watch out for him.  ||| Esa nanny es hella estricta, mira por él. 
That nanny retired early, good for him.  ||| Que la niña se retiró temprano, bueno para él. 
He enjoys his work as a nanny.  ||| Él disfruta de su trabajo como un nanny.
